88:/**
89: * Thin client interface for the e2b SDK methods consumed by this provider.
90: *
91: * Inject a real SDK instance at construction time. When the SDK is installed:
92: *   1. Verify the actual method names and signatures match this interface.
93: *   2. Update or remove this interface — the real SDK types take precedence.
94: *   3. Remove the defaultSdkStub and supply the real client via DI or env.
95: */
96:export interface E2bSdkClient {
97:  /**
98:   * Start a new sandbox from a template alias (digest string).
99:   * Passes wall-clock ceiling as the SDK `timeout` parameter (ms → seconds).
100:   * Returns an opaque sandbox handle with the provider-assigned sandboxId.
101:   */
102:  createSandbox(options: {
103:    templateAlias: string;
104:    timeoutSeconds: number;
105:    metadata: Record<string, string>;
106:  }): Promise<E2bSandboxHandle>;
108:  /**
109:   * Terminate a running sandbox. Idempotent: no-op if sandbox already closed.
110:   */
111:  terminateSandbox(sandboxId: string): Promise<void>;
113:  /**
114:   * Read a file from the sandbox filesystem. Returns a Buffer.
115:   * Throws if the path does not exist or the sandbox is not running.
116:   */
117:  readFile(sandboxId: string, path: string): Promise<Buffer>;
119:  /**
120:   * Write a file to the sandbox filesystem with optional mode.
121:   * Used to inject credential files under /workspace/secrets/.
122:   * Permissions default to 0o600 (owner-read-write) per spec §11.1.
123:   */
124:  writeFile(
125:    sandboxId: string,
126:    path: string,
127:    contents: Buffer,
128:    options?: { mode?: number },
129:  ): Promise<void>;
131:  /**
132:   * List files in a directory inside the sandbox filesystem.
133:   * Returns an empty array when the directory does not exist.
134:   */
135:  listFiles(sandboxId: string, path: string): Promise<E2bFileInfo[]>;
137:  /**
138:   * Read the terminal state of a sandbox.
139:   * Returns the E2bTerminalSignal once the sandbox has exited (any reason).
140:   * Should be called after the sandbox's process has completed.
141:   */
142:  getTerminalState(sandboxId: string): Promise<E2bTerminalSignal>;
144:  /**
145:   * Check whether a sandbox is still alive (running).
146:   * Returns true if the sandbox is reachable and running; false if terminated.
147:   * Used by teardown verification (§7.7 REQ #55) — called after terminateSandbox
148:   * to confirm the sandbox is actually gone.
149:   *
150:   * NOTE: method name must be verified against the real e2b SDK surface at
151:   * installation time. If the real SDK uses a different name, update this
152:   * interface and the defaultSdkStub accordingly.
153:   */
154:  isSandboxAlive(sandboxId: string): Promise<boolean>;
155:}
157:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
158:// Default stub (throws on any call — boot-time silent, first-call loud)
159:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
161:function makeNotInstalledStub(): E2bSdkClient {
162:  const notInstalled = (): never => {
163:    throw new Error(
164:      'e2b SDK not yet installed — see SANDBOX-DEF-EGRESS-MECH decision in C9. ' +
165:        'Install the e2b package and inject a real E2bSdkClient at E2bSandbox construction.',
166:    );
167:  };
168:  return {
169:    createSandbox: notInstalled,
170:    terminateSandbox: notInstalled,
171:    readFile: notInstalled,
172:    writeFile: notInstalled,
173:    listFiles: notInstalled,
174:    getTerminalState: notInstalled,
175:    // Teardown verification stub: returns false (not alive) when SDK not installed.
176:    // The real SDK implementation must be verified at installation time.
177:    isSandboxAlive: async (_sandboxId: string) => false,
178:  };
179:}
181:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
182:// E2bSandbox configuration
183:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
185:export interface E2bSandboxConfig {
186:  /**
187:   * e2b project name — 'synthetos-prod' or 'synthetos-staging'.
188:   * Read from E2B_PROJECT_PROD / E2B_PROJECT_STAGING env vars by the default
189:   * factory registered at module init. Tests or custom bootstrap inject directly.
190:   */
191:  projectName: string;
193:  /**
194:   * Path to the synthetos-sandbox PUBLISHED_VERSION file.
195:   * Default: 'infra/sandbox-templates/synthetos-sandbox/PUBLISHED_VERSION'
196:   * relative to process.cwd(). Overridable for tests.
197:   */
198:  publishedVersionPath: string;
200:  /**
201:   * Path to the iee-browser PUBLISHED_VERSION file.
202:   * When set, enables browser-class sandbox execution (templateName = 'iee-browser').
203:   * Default: 'infra/sandbox-templates/iee-browser/PUBLISHED_VERSION'
204:   * relative to process.cwd().
205:   */
206:  browserPublishedVersionPath?: string;
207:}
209:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
210:// E2bSandbox — the provider implementation
211:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
213:export class E2bSandbox implements SandboxExecutionService {
214:  private readonly sdkClient: E2bSdkClient;
215:  private readonly config: E2bSandboxConfig;
216:  private readonly templateDigest: string;
217:  private readonly browserTemplateDigest: string | null;
219:  constructor(sdkClient: E2bSdkClient, config: E2bSandboxConfig) {
220:    this.sdkClient = sdkClient;
221:    this.config = config;
223:    // Resolve the immutable template digest from PUBLISHED_VERSION at
224:    // construction time (spec §15.3). This makes every subsequent runTask
225:    // call use the same pinned digest — consistent with the one-sandbox-per-
226:    // task, no-pooling-no-reuse contract (§8.2.1).
227:    const rawText = readFileSync(config.publishedVersionPath, 'utf-8');
228:    const published = parsePublishedVersion(rawText);
230:    assertNotLatestTemplateVersion(published.image_digest, 'E2bSandbox.constructor');
231:    this.templateDigest = published.image_digest;
233:    // Load iee-browser template digest if configured (enables browser-class tasks).
234:    if (config.browserPublishedVersionPath) {
235:      const browserRaw = readFileSync(config.browserPublishedVersionPath, 'utf-8');
236:      const browserPublished = parsePublishedVersion(browserRaw);
237:      assertNotLatestTemplateVersion(browserPublished.image_digest, 'E2bSandbox.constructor(browser)');
238:      this.browserTemplateDigest = browserPublished.image_digest;
239:    } else {
240:      this.browserTemplateDigest = null;
241:    }
242:  }
244:  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
245:  // runTask — one sandbox per task, no pooling, no reuse (spec §8.2.1)
246:  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
248:  async runTask(input: SandboxRunTaskInput): Promise<SandboxRunTaskOutput> {
249:    const {
250:      sandboxExecutionId,
251:      organisationId,
252:      subaccountId,
253:      runId,
254:      agentId,
255:      taskId,
256:      templateName,
257:      templateVersion,
258:      policy,
259:      credentialIssuanceContext,
260:    } = input;
262:    // Wall-clock ceiling → SDK timeout parameter (ms → seconds, rounded up).
263:    const timeoutSeconds = Math.ceil(policy.ceilings.wallClockMs / 1000);
265:    const makeTelemetryWriter = (): (event: ProviderDiagnosticEvent) => Promise<void> =>
266:      async (event) => {
267:        const db = getOrgScopedDb('e2bSandbox.telemetryWriter');
268:        await allocateAndInsertTelemetryEvent(db, {
269:          sandboxExecutionId,
270:          organisationId,
271:          subaccountId,
272:          runId,
273:          agentId,
274:          taskId,
275:          provider: 'e2b',
276:          templateName,
277:          templateVersion,
278:          eventType: 'provider_diagnostic',
279:          criticality: 'info',
280:          payloadJson: {
281:            subKind: event.subKind,
282:            attempt: event.attempt,
283:            elapsedMs: event.elapsedMs,
284:            status: event.status,
285:            code: event.code,
286:          },
287:        });
288:      };
290:    const metadataTags = buildE2bMetadataTags({
291:      organisationId,
292:      subaccountId,
293:      runId,
294:      agentId,
295:      taskId,
296:      sandboxExecutionId,
297:      templateName,
298:      templateVersion,
299:    });
301:    // --- Phase: start ---
302:    // Warm-pool adoption: if a leased provider sandbox id is supplied, use it
303:    // directly and skip createSandbox(). This is the whole point of the
304:    // warm-pool lease — the sandbox was pre-created by refillIfEligible.
305:    // Cold-start dispatches (no lease) fall through to createSandbox.
306:    let providerSandboxId: string;
307:    if (input.leasedProviderSandboxId) {
308:      providerSandboxId = input.leasedProviderSandboxId;
309:    } else {
310:      const handle = await withSandboxProvider({
311:        phase: 'start',
312:        sandboxExecutionId,
313:        telemetryWriter: makeTelemetryWriter(),
314:        call: () =>
315:          this.sdkClient.createSandbox({
316:            templateAlias: resolveTemplateAlias(templateName, {
317:              synthetos: this.templateDigest,
318:              browser: this.browserTemplateDigest ?? undefined,
319:            }),
320:            timeoutSeconds,
321:            metadata: metadataTags,
322:          }),
323:      });
324:      providerSandboxId = handle.sandboxId;
325:    }
327:    // --- Phase: credential injection (spec §11) ---
328:    // Write each credential alias under /workspace/secrets/{alias}.token at
329:    // 0600 permissions. The caller (sandboxExecutionService / adapter) has
330:    // already issued credentials via credentialBrokerService; the values
331:    // arrive through credentialIssuanceContext.
332:    // In V1 this stub writes no actual files (credential values are not yet
333:    // threaded through the input descriptor — that wiring is C13's concern).
334:    // The per-execution redaction pattern set (§11.3) is assembled by the
335:    // harvest pipeline (C7); this provider does not manage redaction patterns.
336:    for (const alias of credentialIssuanceContext.aliases) {
337:      const targetPath = credentialAliasPath(alias.alias);
338:      // Credential value is not available in the input descriptor in V1.
339:      // C13 (adapter rewiring) threads the issued credential value through.
340:      // When available: this.sdkClient.writeFile(providerSandboxId, targetPath,
341:      //   Buffer.from(credentialValue), { mode: 0o600 });
342:      void (alias.alias + targetPath); // suppress lint unused-var until C13 wires
343:    }
345:    // --- Phase: harness input injection (browser tasks only) ---
346:    // For iee-browser tasks, write /workspace/input.json so the harness can
347:    // read the task payload and profile mount descriptor at startup.
348:    // The harness uses profileMount.userDataDirInSandbox to set up the
349:    // Playwright user-data directory (spec §7.3, §8.1 extension).
350:    //
351:    // The task envelope (URL, actions, contract, etc.) is threaded through
352:    // `input.browserTaskPayload` (NOT `inputFiles` — inputFiles is for file
353:    // attachments). The harness validates the envelope it expects.
354:    //
355:    // Note: the sandbox is already running when this write happens, so the
356:    // harness entrypoint must wait for /workspace/input.json before launching
357:    // (see entrypoint.sh wait-loop, 30s default).
358:    if (templateName === 'iee-browser' && input.profileMount) {
359:      // proxy alignment: resolved by proxyAlignmentService.resolve at dispatch time
360:      // when PROXY_ALIGNMENT=true and the subaccount has a proxyConfig configured.
361:      // proxyUrlEnvKey names the env var (set by credentialBrokerService.injectIntoEnvironment)
362:      // holding the credential-resolved proxy URL. Credentials never appear in taskPayload.
363:      // Full wiring (DB read of proxy_config + locale_overrides → resolve call) is threaded
364:      // in the IEE dispatch layer when the proxy-config UI and credential-broker integration land.
365:      const proxyAlignment: ProxyAlignment | null = input.proxyAlignment ?? null;
366:      const proxyUrlEnvKey: string | null = input.proxyUrlEnvKey ?? null;
367:      // HUMANIZE_ENABLED gates the feature flag. When off, the envelope carries null
368:      // regardless of what the caller supplied (workflow.humanize or input.humanize).
369:      // The dispatch-layer caller reads workflowDefinition.humanize and threads it
370:      // through input.humanize; this provider enforces the flag at envelope assembly.
371:      const humanizeEnabled = process.env['HUMANIZE_ENABLED'] === 'true';
372:      const humanize: HumanizeOptions | null = humanizeEnabled ? (input.humanize ?? null) : null;
373:      // browser-vision-grounding spec §8.2/§8.3: thread the four vision fields
374:      // into /workspace/input.json so the harness can route to visionDecisionLoop
375:      // when decisionMode is 'vision' or 'hybrid'. Without this propagation the
376:      // harness always sees decisionMode=absent and defaults to 'dom', making
377:      // the entire vision dispatch path dead-code at the boundary.
378:      // visionEndpointToken is a short-lived secret — token-redaction contract
379:      // (spec §8.3) applies once the follow-up harness implementation lands.
380:      const harnessInput = {
381:        taskPayload: input.browserTaskPayload ?? null,
382:        profileMount: {
383:          userDataDirInSandbox: input.profileMount.userDataDirInSandbox,
384:        },
385:        artefactsDir: '/workspace/artefacts',
386:        proxyAlignment,
387:        proxyUrlEnvKey,
388:        humanize,
389:        decisionMode: input.decisionMode ?? null,
390:        visionEndpointUrl: input.visionEndpointUrl ?? null,
391:        visionEndpointToken: input.visionEndpointToken ?? null,
392:        visionModelId: input.visionModelId ?? null,
393:      };
394:      await withSandboxProvider({
395:        phase: 'start',
396:        sandboxExecutionId,
397:        telemetryWriter: makeTelemetryWriter(),
398:        call: () =>
399:          this.sdkClient.writeFile(
400:            providerSandboxId,
401:            '/workspace/input.json',
402:            Buffer.from(JSON.stringify(harnessInput)),
403:          ),
404:      });
405:    }
407:    // --- Phase: mid_execution / terminal harvest ---
408:    // The harvest pipeline runs inline within runTask (spec §22).
409:    // Steps 1-12 per spec §8.4 are owned by sandboxHarvestService (C7), which
410:    // is invoked by sandboxExecutionService (C5). This provider's responsibility
411:    // is to:
412:    //   (a) read the terminal state via the SDK
413:    //   (b) read /workspace/output.json, /workspace/artefacts/, /workspace/logs/
414:    //   (c) terminate the sandbox when done
415:    //   (d) surface a typed SandboxRunTaskOutput
416:    //
417:    // In V1 the harvest pipeline (C7) is separate: sandboxExecutionService calls
418:    // sandboxHarvestService.runHarvest(input, providerAdapter). This method
419:    // returns a minimal output representing the raw provider result before
420:    // the full harvest pipeline processes it. C5 orchestrates the full flow.
422:    const terminalSignal = await withSandboxProvider({
423:      phase: 'terminal',
424:      sandboxExecutionId,
425:      telemetryWriter: makeTelemetryWriter(),
426:      call: () => this.sdkClient.getTerminalState(providerSandboxId),
427:    });
429:    const terminalState = e2bTerminalSignalToInternal(terminalSignal);
431:    // Read output.json from the sandbox filesystem.
432:    let rawOutput: unknown | null = null;
433:    if (terminalState === 'completed' || terminalState === 'crashed') {
434:      // Attempt output read even on crash — harvest pipeline classifies the
435:      // result. Provider reads are wrapped for retry / signal classification.
436:      try {
437:        const outputBuf = await withSandboxProvider({
438:          phase: 'harvest',
439:          sandboxExecutionId,
440:          telemetryWriter: makeTelemetryWriter(),
441:          call: () => this.sdkClient.readFile(providerSandboxId, '/workspace/output.json'),
442:        });
443:        rawOutput = JSON.parse(outputBuf.toString('utf-8')) as unknown;
444:      } catch (err) {
445:        // Missing or unreadable output.json — harvest pipeline classifies this
446:        // as output_validation_failed. rawOutput stays null.
447:        logger.warn('sandbox.e2b.output_read_failed', {
448:          sandboxExecutionId,
449:          err: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
450:        });
451:      }
452:    }
454:    // Read log files.
455:    const logRefs = await this._harvestLogs(providerSandboxId, sandboxExecutionId);
457:    // Enumerate and upload artefacts (stub — full wiring in C7).
458:    const artefactRefs = await this._harvestArtefacts(providerSandboxId, sandboxExecutionId);
460:    // Terminate the sandbox. Idempotent — no-op if already closed.
461:    await withSandboxProvider({
462:      phase: 'harvest',
463:      sandboxExecutionId,
464:      telemetryWriter: makeTelemetryWriter(),
465:      call: () => this.sdkClient.terminateSandbox(providerSandboxId),
466:    }).catch((err: unknown) => {
467:      // Terminate failure is non-fatal: the sandbox may already be closed
468:      // (timeout, cost-ceiling), or the provider API is temporarily down.
469:      // The ceiling-monitor job (C11a) and the wall-clock-kill job (C11a)
470:      // both terminate independently as belt-and-braces.
471:      logger.warn('sandbox.e2b.terminate_failed', {
472:        sandboxExecutionId,
473:        err: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
474:      });
475:    });
477:    // Post-terminate verification (§7.7 REQ #55). Runs even if terminate above
478:    // threw — health-check throw maps to verified:false/health_check_threw.
479:    const verification = await verifyTeardown({
480:      providerSandboxId,
481:      postTerminateHealthCheck: () => this.sdkClient.isSandboxAlive(providerSandboxId),
482:    });
484:    if (verification.verified) {
485:      logger.info('sandbox.teardown.verified', { providerSandboxId });
486:    } else {
487:      logger.error('sandbox.teardown.unverified', {
488:        providerSandboxId,
489:        reason: verification.reason,
490:      });
491:    }
493:    // Metrics: populated from provider-reported data where available.
494:    // In V1 the e2b SDK surface for per-execution vCPU / memory metrics is
495:    // unknown until the real SDK is installed. Stubs carry wall-clock only.
496:    const metrics: SandboxExecutionMetrics = {
497:      wallClockMs: policy.ceilings.wallClockMs, // provider-reported not yet available
498:      vcpuSeconds: 0,
499:      peakMemoryMb: 0,
500:      egressBytes: 0,
501:    };
503:    // Cost: provider-reported at harvest time. Stubbed at 0 until the real
504:    // SDK exposes a cost API (see SANDBOX-DEF-EGRESS-MECH decision).
505:    const costCents = 0;
507:    return {
508:      sandboxExecutionId,
509:      terminalState,
510:      output: terminalState === 'completed' ? rawOutput : null,
511:      artefactRefs,
512:      logRefs,
513:      metrics,
514:      costCents,
515:      templateName,
516:      templateVersion,
517:      provider: 'e2b',
518:    };
519:  }
521:  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
522:  // terminate — kill a running sandbox by its provider-assigned id.
523:  // Idempotent: no-op if the sandbox is already closed.
524:  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
526:  async terminate(providerSandboxId: string): Promise<void> {
527:    await this.sdkClient.terminateSandbox(providerSandboxId);
529:    const verification = await verifyTeardown({
530:      providerSandboxId,
531:      postTerminateHealthCheck: () => this.sdkClient.isSandboxAlive(providerSandboxId),
532:    });
534:    if (verification.verified) {
535:      logger.info('sandbox.teardown.verified', { providerSandboxId });
536:    } else {
537:      logger.error('sandbox.teardown.unverified', {
538:        providerSandboxId,
539:        reason: verification.reason,
540:      });
541:    }
542:  }
544:  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
545:  // Log harvest (stub — full wiring in C7 harvest pipeline)
546:  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
548:  private async _harvestLogs(
549:    providerSandboxId: string,
550:    sandboxExecutionId: string,
551:  ): Promise<SandboxLogRefs> {
552:    const readLog = async (stream: 'stdout' | 'stderr'): Promise<string> => {
553:      try {
554:        // no-tenancy-context: defaults to log-only. This private method takes only
555:        // (providerSandboxId, sandboxExecutionId) — the full tenancy fields required
556:        // by sandbox_telemetry_events (organisationId, runId, agentId, taskId,
557:        // templateName, templateVersion) are not threaded here. Diagnostics surface
558:        // via logger.warn in withSandboxProvider only; DB-row persistence at this
559:        // site requires a method-signature refactor and is tracked in tasks/todo.md
560:        // under REQ #31 follow-up.
561:        await withSandboxProvider({
562:          phase: 'harvest',
563:          sandboxExecutionId,
564:          call: () =>
565:            this.sdkClient.readFile(providerSandboxId, `/workspace/logs/${stream}.log`),
566:        });
567:        // C7 (harvest pipeline) processes the raw buffer through redaction and
568:        // persists to sandbox_logs. This stub returns an opaque log-ref string.
569:      } catch (err) {
570:        logger.warn('sandbox.e2b.log_harvest_read_failed', {
571:          sandboxExecutionId,
572:          providerSandboxId,
573:          stream,
574:          err: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
575:        });
576:      }
577:      return `e2b:${sandboxExecutionId}:${stream}`;
578:    };
580:    return {
581:      stdout: await readLog('stdout'),
582:      stderr: await readLog('stderr'),
583:    };
584:  }
586:  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
587:  // Artefact harvest (stub — full wiring in C7 harvest pipeline)
588:  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
590:  private async _harvestArtefacts(
591:    providerSandboxId: string,
592:    sandboxExecutionId: string,
593:  ): Promise<SandboxArtefactRef[]> {
594:    try {
595:      // no-tenancy-context: defaults to log-only. This private method takes only
596:      // (providerSandboxId, sandboxExecutionId) — the full tenancy fields required
597:      // by sandbox_telemetry_events (organisationId, runId, agentId, taskId,
598:      // templateName, templateVersion) are not threaded here. Diagnostics surface
599:      // via logger.warn in withSandboxProvider only; DB-row persistence at this
600:      // site requires a method-signature refactor and is tracked in tasks/todo.md
601:      // under REQ #31 follow-up.
602:      const entries = await withSandboxProvider({
603:        phase: 'harvest',
604:        sandboxExecutionId,
605:        call: () => this.sdkClient.listFiles(providerSandboxId, '/workspace/artefacts'),
606:      });
608:      // C7 handles: per-artefact size check (§9.4), total-bytes cap, metadata
609:      // redaction (§8.4 step 7), and S3 upload (§8.4 step 8). This stub
610:      // returns an empty list — artefact wiring lands in C7.
611:      void entries;
612:    } catch (err) {
613:      logger.warn('sandbox.e2b.artefact_harvest_list_failed', {
614:        sandboxExecutionId,
615:        providerSandboxId,
616:        err: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
617:      });
618:    }
619:    return [];
620:  }
621:}
623:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
624:// Module-init registration (F1 fix — registration-seam pattern)
625://
626:// Called at module-import time so that C4's resolveSandboxProvider() can find
627:// the 'e2b' constructor without statically importing this file.
628:// The factory reads E2B_PROJECT_PROD / E2B_PROJECT_STAGING from process.env
629:// at construction time (not at module-load time) so tests can override.
630:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
632:registerSandboxProvider('e2b', () => {
633:  const nodeEnv = process.env['NODE_ENV'] ?? 'development';
634:  const stubAllowed = process.env['E2B_SDK_STUBBED'] === 'true';
636:  // Fail-fast guard: the e2b SDK is not installed yet. Refusing to construct
637:  // an e2b provider when the SDK is absent prevents the resolver from handing
638:  // back a provider that "looks valid" at boot but throws on first real call.
639:  // Tests construct E2bSandbox directly with an injected client and never
640:  // reach this factory. Local / dev work that wants the not-installed stub
641:  // must opt in explicitly via E2B_SDK_STUBBED=true; production NEVER opts in.
642:  if (nodeEnv === 'production' || !stubAllowed) {
643:    throw new FailureError(
644:      failure(
645:        'sandbox_provider_unavailable',
646:        nodeEnv === 'production'
647:          ? 'e2b SDK is not installed — production cannot use the not-installed stub; install the SDK and inject a real client before setting SANDBOX_PROVIDER=e2b'
648:          : 'e2b SDK is not installed — set E2B_SDK_STUBBED=true to use the not-installed stub in non-production, or install the SDK and inject a real client at module init',
649:        { nodeEnv, sdkInstalled: false, stubAllowed },
650:      ),
651:    );
652:  }
654:  const projectEnvKey =
655:    nodeEnv === 'production' ? 'E2B_PROJECT_PROD' : 'E2B_PROJECT_STAGING';
656:  const projectName = process.env[projectEnvKey];
658:  if (!projectName) {
659:    throw new FailureError(
660:      failure(
661:        'sandbox_provider_unavailable',
662:        `${projectEnvKey} env var is not set — required for e2b sandbox provider`,
663:        { projectEnvKey, nodeEnv },
664:      ),
665:    );
666:  }
668:  const publishedVersionPath = join(
669:    process.cwd(),
670:    'infra',
671:    'sandbox-templates',
672:    'synthetos-sandbox',
673:    'PUBLISHED_VERSION',
674:  );
676:  // Browser template loading is gated behind E2B_BROWSER_TEMPLATE_ENABLED.
677:  // The committed iee-browser/PUBLISHED_VERSION carries a placeholder
678:  // (all-zero) image_digest until the CI sandbox-template-build pipeline
679:  // publishes a real one (see SANDBOX-DEF-EGRESS-MECH). Without the gate,
680:  // assertNotLatestTemplateVersion rejects the placeholder and blocks the
681:  // synthetos-sandbox provider from constructing in dev — even though dev
682:  // only needs the base template.
683:  const browserTemplateEnabled = process.env['E2B_BROWSER_TEMPLATE_ENABLED'] === 'true';
684:  const browserPublishedVersionPath = browserTemplateEnabled
685:    ? join(
686:        process.cwd(),
687:        'infra',
688:        'sandbox-templates',
689:        'iee-browser',
690:        'PUBLISHED_VERSION',
691:      )
692:    : undefined;
694:  return new E2bSandbox(makeNotInstalledStub(), {
695:    projectName,
696:    publishedVersionPath,
697:    browserPublishedVersionPath,
698:  });
699:});
